];

function getNavItems(userType: string | undefined, role: string | undefined) {
  if (role === 'admin' || userType === 'admin') return adminNavItems;
  if (userType === 'enterprise') return enterpriseNavItems;
  return jobseekerNavItems;
}

function getHomeRoute(userType: string | undefined, role: string | undefined) {
  if (role === 'admin' || userType === 'admin') return '/admin/users';
  if (userType === 'enterprise') return '/enterprise/home';
  return '/jobseeker/home';
}

AgentThinkAction(thought='Found the root cause! \n\nThe `has_role` function queries the `profiles` table itself:\n```sql\nSELECT EXISTS (\n  SELECT 1 FROM profiles p WHERE p.id = uid AND p.role = role_name::user_role\n);\n```\n\nAnd there\'s a policy "管理员可完全访问profiles" that uses `has_role()` - this creates a **circular RLS dependency**:\n\n1. User queries `profiles` table\n2. RLS policy "管理员可完全访问profiles" calls `has_role()`\n3. `has_role()` queries `profiles` table again\n4. Which triggers RLS again → infinite recursion!\n\nThis infinite recursion causes the `fetchProfile` query to hang indefinitely, which is why the login button stays "登录中..." forever.\n\nThe fix: The `has_role` function needs to use `SECURITY DEFINER` or bypass RLS, OR the admin policy should use a different approach (like `auth.uid()` directly checking a JWT claim, or using `SET search_path` tricks).\n\nThe simplest fix: make the `has_role` function `SECURITY DEFINER` so it bypasses RLS when querying profiles. Or alternatively, rewrite the admin policy to not use `has_role` but instead directly check using a subquery that bypasses RLS.\n\nActually, using `SECURITY DEFINER` on the helper function is the correct approach per the guidelines. Let me fix the `has_role` function to be `SECURITY DEFINER`.\n\nAlso there\'s another issue: the policy "所有认证用户可查看公开profile" has `qual: true` - this means all authenticated users can SELECT from profiles. This policy alone should allow fetchProfile to work without hitting the recursive policy. But maybe the admin ALL policy is evaluated first and causes the recursion.\n\nActually, RLS policies are evaluated with OR - if ANY policy allows access, the row is accessible. The "所有认证用户可查看公开profile" SELECT policy with `qual: true` should be sufficient for SELECT. But maybe the "管理员可完全访问profiles" ALL policy with its recursive call is causing a stack overflow/deadlock that prevents any query from completing.\n\nThe fix: \n1. Make `has_role` SECURITY DEFINER so it bypasses RLS\n2. This breaks the infinite recursion\n\nLet me also check: does the `uid()` function exist? THOUGHT: 找到根本原因了！**RLS 策略循环递归**：

- `profiles` 表有一条管理员策略调用了 `has_role()` 函数
- `has_role()` 函数内部又查询了 `profiles` 表
- 这导致无限递归 → 查询永久挂起 → 按钮卡在"登录中..."

**问题根因**：`profiles` 表的管理员 RLS 策略调用 `has_role()` 函数，该函数又反过来查询 `profiles` 表，触发 RLS，形成**无限递归**。数据库查询永远不返回，导致登录后 `fetchProfile` 永久挂起，按钮卡在"登录中..."。

**修复方案**：为 `has_role()` 函数添加 `SECURITY DEFINER` + `SET search_path = public`，让函数以定义者权限执行，绕过 RLS 检查，打破递归循环。现在刷新页面重新登录即可正常进入系统。
</action>

    58     e.preventDefault();
    59     if (!agreed) return;
    60     if (!regUsername || !regPassword || !regDisplayName) return;
    61     if (regUserType === 'enterprise' && !regCompanyName) return;

    67         display_name: regDisplayName,
    68         user_type: regUserType,
    69         company_name: regCompanyName,
    70       });
    71       // 注册成功后自动登录
    72       await login(regUsername, regPassword);
    73     } finally {
    74       setRegLoading(false);
    75     }

const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | undefined>(undefined);

/** 从 auth.User 元数据中构建兜底 profile，避免 fetchProfile 失败时用户卡在登录页 */
function buildFallbackProfile(authUser: User): Profile {
  const meta = authUser.user_metadata ?? {};
  const email = authUser.email ?? '';
  const username = meta.username ?? email.split('@')[0] ?? authUser.id;
  return {
    id: authUser.id,
    username,
    email,
    display_name: meta.display_name ?? username,
    user_type: meta.user_type ?? 'jobseeker',
    role: meta.role ?? 'user',
    avatar_url: meta.avatar_url ?? null,
    bio: null,
    location: null,
    website: null,
    phone: null,
    created_at: authUser.created_at ?? new Date().toISOString(),
    updated_at: authUser.updated_at ?? new Date().toISOString(),
  } as Profile;
}
```

**MessageAction** (source=EventSource.AGENT)
CONTENT: 0 错误，修复完成。总结一下本次修复的两个问题：

---

**问题一：navigate 在 render 函数体内调用（React 反模式）**

原代码在组件 render 阶段直接调用 `navigate()`，这在 React 并发渲染下会导致不可预期的行为（可能被跳过或中断）。已改为在 `useEffect` 中监听 `isAuthenticated + user` 变化后再执行跳转。

**问题二：fetchProfile 返回 null 时用户永远卡在登录页**

如果 `profiles` 表查询因任何原因（RLS、网络、数据缺失）返回 `null`，`setUser(null)` 导致 `isAuthenticated` 始终为 false，登录永远不会跳转。已添加 `buildFallbackProfile` 兜底逻辑：当 profile 查不到时，自动从 Supabase Auth 的用户元数据构建一个临时 profile，确保登录后能正常进入系统。
</action>

Makes the HTTP POST to auth/v1/token → 200 OK\n2. Internally processes the response (stores session, etc.)\n3. Triggers `onAuthStateChange` with SIGNED_IN\n4. Returns `{ data, error }`\n\nStep 3 happens asynchronously inside the Supabase client. The `onAuthStateChange` callback fires. Our callback:\n```js\nasync (event, s) => {\n  setSession(s);\n  if (s?.user) {\n    const profile = await fetchProfile(s.user.id);  // THIS HANGS!\n    setUser(profile ?? buildFallbackProfile(s.user));\n  }\n  ...\n}\n```\n\n`fetchProfile` hangs (no HTTP request to profiles). This means the callback awaits forever. \n\nBut HERE\'S THE CRITICAL INSIGHT: In older versions of Supabase JS client, `onAuthStateChange` callbacks were synchronous. In newer versions (v2), they may be awaited before `signInWithPassword` resolves!\n\nIf the Supabase client v2 AWAITS the `onAuthStateChange` callback before resolving `signInWithPassword`, then:\n1. `signInWithPassword` → 200 OK\n2. Client awaits onAuthStateChange callback\n3. Callback calls `fetchProfile` which hangs\n4. `signInWithPassword` never resolves\n5. `handleLogin` never hits the `finally` block\n6. `loginLoading` stays true\n7. Button stays "登录中..."\n\nThis is exactly what we\'re seeing! The Supabase v2 client DOES await async `onAuthStateChange` callbacks before resolving auth calls.\n\nThe fix: **Make the `onAuthStateChange` callback non-blocking** - don\'t use `async/await` inside it. Instead, fire-and-forget the profile fetch.\n\nActually - the correct fix is to NOT use async in the onAuthStateChange callback, or to ensure the profile fetch doesn\'t block it.\n\nLet me fix the AuthContext to use a fire-and-forget pattern for fetchProfile inside onAuthStateChange.\n\nActually - looking at the Supabase JS v2 docs: "The callback should not return a promise" - async callbacks in onAuthStateChange can block the auth flow!\n\nThe fix:\n```js\nsupabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((event, s) => {\n  setSession(s);\n  if (s?.user) {\n    // Fire and forget - don\'t await\n    fetchProfile(s.user.id).then(profile => {\n      setUser(profile ?? buildFallbackProfile(s.user));\n    });\n  } else {\n    setUser(null);\n  }\n  if (event === \'SIGNED_IN\') {\n    setIsLoading(false);\n  }\n});\n```\n\nThis way, the callback returns synchronously and doesn\'t block signInWithPassword from resolving. The profile fetch happens asynchronously.\n\nBut there\'s a subtle issue: if we set `setIsLoading(false)` before the profile is fetched, the UI might briefly show the loading state. Let me think...\n\nActually for the login flow:\n1. onAuthStateChange fires → callback returns synchronously → signInWithPassword resolves\n2. handleLogin\'s finally: setLoginLoading(false) → button back to "登录"\n3. Separately, fetchProfile completes → setUser(profile) → isAuthenticated becomes true\n4. useEffect in Login.tsx: navigate to appropriate page\n\nThis flow works! Thought: 找到真正原因了！**Supabase JS v2 的 `onAuthStateChange` 如果传入 `async` 回调，客户端会等待它完成才让 `signInWithPassword` resolve**。我们的回调里 `await fetchProfile(...)` 挂起 → 整个 `login()` 永不返回 → 按钮永远显示"登录中..."。

Command: str_replace
Old String: ```

     1 import React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState, useCallback } from 'react';
     2 import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     3 import { AuthContextType, Profile, RegisterData } from '@/types/types';
     4 import { toast } from 'sonner';
     5 import { User } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
     6 
     7 const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | undefined>(undefined);
     8 
     9 /** 从 auth.User 元数据中构建兜底 profile，避免 fetchProfile 失败时用户卡在登录页 */
    10 function buildFallbackProfile(authUser: User): Profile {
    11   const meta = authUser.user_metadata ?? {};
    12   const email = authUser.email ?? '';
    13   const username = meta.username ?? email.split('@')[0] ?? authUser.id;
    14   return {
    15     id: authUser.id,
    16     username,
    17     email,
    18     display_name: meta.display_name ?? username,
    19     user_type: meta.user_type ?? 'jobseeker',
    20     role: meta.role ?? 'user',
    21     avatar_url: meta.avatar_url ?? null,
    22     bio: null,
    23     location: null,
    24     website: null,
    25     phone: null,
    26     created_at: authUser.created_at ?? new Date().toISOString(),
    27     updated_at: authUser.updated_at ?? new Date().toISOString(),
    28   } as unknown as Profile;
    29 }
    30 
    31 export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
    32   const [user, setUser] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
    33   const [session, setSession] = useState<unknown>(null);
    34   const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
    35 
    36   const fetchProfile = useCallback(async (userId: string) => {
    37     const { data, error } = await supabase
    38       .from('profiles')
    39       .select('*')
    40       .eq('id', userId)
    41       .maybeSingle();
    42     if (error) {
    43       console.error('获取用户信息失败:', error);
    44       return null;
    45     }
    46     return data as Profile | null;
    47   }, []);
    48 
    49   const refreshProfile = useCallback(async () => {
    50     const { data: { session: currentSession } } = await supabase.auth.getSession();
    51     if (currentSession?.user) {
    52       const profile = await fetchProfile(currentSession.user.id);
    53       setUser(profile);
    54     }
    55   }, [fetchProfile]);
    56 
    57   useEffect(() => {
    58     // 初始化获取session
    59     supabase.auth.getSession().then(({ data: { session: s } }) => {
    60       setSession(s);
    61       if (s?.user) {
    62         fetchProfile(s.user.id).then(profile => {
    63           setUser(profile ?? buildFallbackProfile(s.user!));
    64           setIsLoading(false);
    65         });
    66       } else {
    67         setIsLoading(false);
    68       }
    69     });
    70 
    71     // 监听auth状态变化（回调必须是同步的，异步 await 会阻塞 signInWithPassword 返回）
    72     const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((event, s) => {
    73       setSession(s);
    74       if (s?.user) {
    75         // 用 .then() 异步更新 profile，不阻塞 auth 回调
    76         fetchProfile(s.user.id).then(profile => {
    77           setUser(profile ?? buildFallbackProfile(s.user!));
    78         });
    79       } else {
    80         setUser(null);
    81       }
    82       if (event === 'SIGNED_IN') {
    83         setIsLoading(false);
    84       }
    85     });
    86 
    87     return () => subscription.unsubscribe();
    88   }, [fetchProfile]);
    89 
    90   const login = async (username: string, password: string) => {
    91     const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
    92     const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
    93     if (error) {
    94       toast.error('登录失败：' + (error.message.includes('Invalid') ? '用户名或密码错误' : error.message));
    95       throw error;
    96     }
    97     toast.success('登录成功');
    98   };
    99 
   100   const register = async (data: RegisterData) => {
   101     const email = `${data.username}@miaoda.com`;
   102     const { data: authData, error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
   103       email,
   104       password: data.password,
   105       options: {
   106         data: {
   107           username: data.username,
   108           display_name: data.display_name,
   109           user_type: data.user_type,
   110         }
   111       }
   112     });
   113     if (error) {
   114       if (error.message.includes('already registered') || error.message.includes('unique')) {
   115         toast.error('注册失败：用户名已存在');
   116       } else {
   117         toast.error('注册失败：' + error.message);
   118       }
   119       throw error;
   120     }
   121 
   122     // 如果是企业用户，创建企业信息
   123     if (data.user_type === 'enterprise' && data.company_name && authData.user) {
   124       await supabase.from('enterprise_profiles').insert({
   125         profile_id: authData.user.id,
   126         company_name: data.company_name,
   127       });
   128     }
   129 
   130     toast.success('注册成功，欢迎加入！');
   131   };
   132 
   133   const logout = async () => {
   134     await supabase.auth.signOut();
   135     setUser(null);
   136     setSession(null);
   137     toast.success('已退出登录');
   138   };
   139 
   140   const value: AuthContextType = {
   141     user,
   142     session,
   143     isLoading,
   144     isAuthenticated: !!user,
   145     login,
   146     register,
   147     logout,
   148     refreshProfile,
   149   };
   150 
   151   return <AuthContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</AuthContext.Provider>;
   152 }
   153 
   154 export function useAuth() {
   155   const context = useContext(AuthContext);
   156   if (!context) {
   157     throw new Error('useAuth 必须在 AuthProvider 内部使用');
   158   }
   159   return context;
   160 }

<action>
**MessageAction** (source=EventSource.AGENT)
CONTENT: 修复完成。**根本原因**：

Supabase JS v2 的 `onAuthStateChange` 如果传入 `async` 回调，会**等待该 Promise 完成才让 `signInWithPassword` resolve**。我们的 `async` 回调里 `await fetchProfile()` 因 RLS 递归问题一直挂起，导致整条链路死锁：

```
signInWithPassword → 等待 onAuthStateChange 回调 → 等待 fetchProfile → [挂起]
                                                                         ↑永远不返回
```

**修复方案**：将 `onAuthStateChange` 改为同步回调，profile 查询改用 `.then()` 异步处理。这样：
1. auth 回调立即同步返回 → `signInWithPassword` 正常 resolve → 按钮恢复
2. profile 在后台异步加载 → 完成后触发 `useEffect` 中的 navigate → 成功跳转
</action>

So for INSERT, the row must satisfy `sender_id = uid() OR receiver_id = uid()`. Let me check the syntax...\n\nActually the syntax for nested AND in OR should be:\n`.or(`sender_id.eq.${userId},receiver_id.eq.${contactId}`)` - but this isn\'t right, we need to filter for conversations BETWEEN two specific people.\n\nThe correct syntax is:\n```js\n.or(`and(sender_id.eq.${user!.id},receiver_id.eq.${contactId}),and(sender_id.eq.${contactId},receiver_id.eq.${user!.id})`)\n```\n\nThis is the correct Supabase v2 syntax. ✓\n\nLet me now rewrite the Messages.tsx to:\n1. | 译文段落                 |\n\n### 失败响应字段\n\n| 字段路径    | 类型   | 说明                           |\n|------------|--------|--------------------------------|\n| `log_id`   | number | 请求日志 ID，用于问题排查      |\n| `error_code` | number | 错误码                       |\n| `error_msg`  | string | 错误描述信息                 |\n\n---\n\n## 生成期用法（Agent 直接调用）\n\n```typescript\nconst apiKey = process.env["INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY"]!; // platform_managed，密钥由平台注入\n\n/**\n * 调用百度翻译通用版 API，将文本从源语言翻译为目标语言。\n * @param q - 待翻译文本，最大 6000 字符\n * @param from - 源语言代码，可设置为 "auto" 自动检测\n * @param to - 目标语言代码，不可设置为 "auto"\n * @returns 翻译结果对象，包含 from、to 和 trans_result 数组\n */\nasync function translateText(\n  q: string,\n  from: string,\n  to: string,\n): Promise<{\n  from: string;\n  to: string;\n }),\n    },\n  );\n\n  if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP error: ${response.status}`);\n\n  const json = await response.json();\n  if (json.error_code) {\n    throw new Error(`API error     67 ## 生成期代码（Agent 直接调用）
    68 
    69 适用于在 Deno 脚本 / 生成期任务中直接调用上游 SSE 流式接口。
    70 
    71 ```typescript
    72 const apiKey = process.env["INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY"]!; // platform_managed 密钥由平台注入
    73 
    74 interface Message {
    75   role: "user" | "assistant" | "system";
    76   content: string;
    77 }
    78 
    79 interface ChatCompletionChunk {
    80   id: string;
    81   choices: Array<{
    82     index: number;
    83     delta: { role?: string; content?: string };
    84     finish_reason: string | null;
    85     flag: number;
    86   }>;
    87 }
    88 
    89 /**
    90  * 调用文心文本生成大模型（流式），将所有增量内容拼接后返回完整回复。
    91  * @param messages - 对话上下文消息数组
    92  * @param enableThinking - 是否开启思考模式，默认 false
    93  * @returns 完整的模型回复文本
    94  */
    95 async function callTextGenerationLLM(
    96   messages: Message[],
    97   enableThinking = false
    98 ): Promise<string> {
    99   const response = await fetch(
   100     "https://app-bhs9a5otro5d-api-zYkZz8qovQ1L-gateway.appmiaoda.com/v2/chat/completions",
   101     {
   102       method: "POST",
   103       headers: {
   104         "Content-Type": "application/json",
   105         "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
   106       },
   107       body: JSON.stringify({ messages, enable_thinking: enableThinking }),
   108     }
   109   );
   110 
   111   if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP error: ${response.status}`);
   112   if (!response.body) throw new Error("No response body");
   113 
   114   const reader = response.body.getReader();
   115   const decoder = new TextDecoder("utf8");
   116   let fullContent = "";
   117   let buffer = "";
   118 
   119   while (true) {
   120     const { done, value } = await reader.read();
   121     if (done) break;
   122 
   123     buffer += decoder.decode(value, { stream: true });
   124     const lines = buffer.split("\n");
   125     buffer = lines.pop() ?? "";
   126 
   127     for (const line of lines) {
   128       if (!line.startsWith("data: ")) continue;
   129       const raw = line.slice(6).trim();
   130       if (raw === "[DONE]") break;
   131       try {
   132         const chunk: ChatCompletionChunk = JSON.parse(raw);
   133         const delta = chunk.choices?.[0]?.delta?.content ?? "";
   134         fullContent += delta;
   135       } catch {
   136         // 跳过无法解析的帧
   137       }
   138     }
   139   }
   140 
   141   return fullContent;
   142 }
   143 
   144 // 使用示例
   145 const reply = await callTextGenerationLLM([
   146   { role: "system", content: "你是一个文本处理助手" },
   147   { role: "user", content: "请将以下内容翻译成英文：人工智能改变世界" },
   148 ]);
   149 console.log(reply);
   150 ```

   154 ## Edge Function 代码（SSE Proxy 模式）
   155 
   156 Edge Function 将上游 SSE 流直接透传给前端，适用于 Web 和 MiniProgram 平台（两者共用同一个 Edge Function）。
   157 
   158 ```typescript
   159 // edge-functions/wenxin-text-generation.ts
   160 const corsHeaders = {
   161   "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
   162   "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type",
   163 };
   164 
   165 Deno.serve(async (req: Request): Promise<Response> => {
   166   // 处理 CORS 预检请求
   167   if (req.method === "OPTIONS") {
   168     return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders });
   169   }
   170 
   171   if (req.method !== "POST") {
   172     return new Response("Method Not Allowed", { status: 405, headers: corsHeaders });
   173   }
   174 
   175   // 1. 解析请求参数
   176   let messages: Array<{ role: string; content: string }>;
   177   let enableThinking = false;
   178 
   179   try {
   180     const body = await req.json();
   181     messages = body.messages;
   182     if (!messages || !Array.isArray(messages) || messages.length === 0) {
   183       throw new Error("Missing or invalid messages");
   184     }
   185     if (body.enable_thinking !== undefined) {
   186       enableThinking = Boolean(body.enable_thinking);
   187     }
   188   } catch (err) {
   189     return new Response(
   190       JSON.stringify({ error: `Invalid request body: ${(err as Error).message}` }),
   191       { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
   192     );
   193   }
   194 
   195   // 2. 读取平台注入的密钥
   196   const apiKey = Deno.env.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY");
   197   if (!apiKey) {
   198     return new Response(
   199       JSON.stringify({ error: "Server configuration error: missing API key" }),
   200       { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
   201     );
   202   }
   203 
   204   // 3. 调用上游 SSE 接口
   205   const upstream = await fetch(
   206     "https://app-bhs9a5otro5d-api-zYkZz8qovQ1L-gateway.appmiaoda.com/v2/chat/completions",
   207     {
   208       method: "POST",
   209       headers: {
   210         "Content-Type": "application/json",
   211         "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
   212       },
   213       body: JSON.stringify({ messages, enable_thinking: enableThinking }),
   214     }
   215   );
   216 
   217   // 转发限流 / 余额不足错误
   218   if (upstream.status === 429 || upstream.status === 402) {
   219     const errText = await upstream.text();
   220     return new Response(errText, {
   221       status: upstream.status,
   222       headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
   223     });
   224   }
   225 
   226   if (!upstream.ok || !upstream.body) {
   227     return new Response(
   228       JSON.stringify({ error: `Upstream error: ${upstream.status}` }),
   229       { status: 502, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
   230     );
   231   }
   232 
   233   // 4. 直接透传 SSE 流，不缓冲
   234   return new Response(upstream.body, {
   235     headers: {
   236       ...corsHeaders,
   237       "Content-Type": "text/event-stream",
   238       "Cache-Control": "no-cache",
   239       "Connection": "keep-alive",
   240       "X-Content-Type-Options": "nosniff",
   241     },
   242   });
   243 });
   244 ```

   248 ## 前端调用代码
   249 
   250 ### Web 平台
   251 
   252 依赖安装：
   253 
   254 ```bash
   255 npm install ky@^1.2.3 eventsource-parser@^3.0.3
   256 # 可选：流式 Markdown 渲染
   257 npm install streamdown@^1.4.0
   258 ```
   259 
   260 **SSE 工具函数（`lib/sse.ts`）：**
   261 
   262 ```typescript
   263 import ky, {
   264   type KyResponse,
   265   type AfterResponseHook,
   266   type NormalizedOptions,
   267 } from "ky";
   268 import { createParser, type EventSourceParser } from "eventsource-parser";
   269 
   270 export interface SSEOptions {
   271   /** 接收到数据帧时的回调 */
   272   onData: (data: string) => void;
   273   /** 接收到事件时的回调（可选） */
   274   onEvent?: (event: unknown) => void;
   275   /** 流式响应完成时的回调（可选） */
   276   onCompleted?: (error?: Error) => void;
   277   /** 请求被中断时的回调（可选） */
   278   onAborted?: () => void;
   279 }
   280 
   281 /**
   282  * 创建 SSE AfterResponseHook，用于处理 ky 的流式响应。
   283  * @param options - SSE 回调选项
   284  * @returns AfterResponseHook
   285  */
   286 export function createSSEHook(options: SSEOptions): AfterResponseHook {
   287   const hook: AfterResponseHook = async (
   288     request: Request,
   289     _options: NormalizedOptions,
   290     response: KyResponse
   291   ) => {
   292     if (!response.ok || !response.body) return;
   293 
   294     let completed = false;
   295     const finish = (error?: Error): void => {
   296       if (completed) return;
   297       completed = true;
   298       options.onCompleted?.(error);
   299     };
   300 
   301     const reader = response.body.getReader();
   302     const decoder = new TextDecoder("utf8");
   303     const parser: EventSourceParser = createParser({
   304       onEvent: (event) => {
   305         if (!event.data) return;
   306         options.onEvent?.(event);
   307         // 处理单 message 多 data 字段的场景
   308         for (const chunk of event.data.split("\\ ")) {
   309           options.onData(chunk);
   310         }
   311       },
   312     });
   313 
   314     const read = (): void => {
   315       reader
   316         .read()
   317         .then((result) => {
   318           if (result.done) {
   319             finish();
   320             return;
   321           }
   322           parser.feed(decoder.decode(result.value, { stream: true }));
   323           read();
   324         })
   325         .catch((error) => {
   326           if (request.signal.aborted) {
   327             options.onAborted?.();
   328             return;
   329           }
   330           finish(error as Error);
   331         });
   332     };
   333 
   334     read();
   335     return response;
   336   };
   337 
   338   return hook;
   339 }
   340 
   341 export interface StreamRequestOptions {
   342   /** Edge Function URL */
   343   functionUrl: string;
   344   /** 请求体 */
   345   requestBody: unknown;
   346   /** Supabase 匿名密钥 */
   347   supabaseAnonKey: string;
   348   /** 接收到每个 SSE 数据帧的回调 */
   349   onData: (data: string) => void;
   350   /** 请求完成回调 */
   351   onComplete: () => void;
   352   /** 错误处理回调 */
   353   onError: (error: Error) => void;
   354   /** 中断信号（可选） */
   355   signal?: AbortSignal;
   356 }
   357 
   358 /**
   359  * 发送流式请求到 Supabase Edge Function。
   360  * @param options - 流式请求选项
   361  */
   362 export async function sendStreamRequest(options: StreamRequestOptions): Promise<void> {
   363   const {
   364     functionUrl,
   365     requestBody,
   366     supabaseAnonKey,
   367     onData,
   368     onComplete,
   369     onError,
   370     signal,
   371   } = options;
   372 
   373   const sseHook = createSSEHook({
   374     onData,
   375     onCompleted: (error?: Error) => {
   376       if (error) onError(error);
   377       else onComplete();
   378     },
   379     onAborted: () => console.log("请求已中断"),
   380   });
   381 
   382   try {
   383     await ky.post(functionUrl, {
   384       json: requestBody,
   385       headers: {
   386         Authorization: `Bearer ${supabaseAnonKey}`,
   387         apikey: supabaseAnonKey,
   388         "Content-Type": "application/json",
   389       },
   390       signal,
   391       hooks: { afterResponse: [sseHook] },
   392     });
   393   } catch (error) {
   394     if (!signal?.aborted) onError(error as Error);
   395   }
   396 }
   397 ```
   398 
   399 **React 组件中使用（Web）：**
   400 
   401 ```typescript
   402 import { useState, useRef } from "react";
   403 import { sendStreamRequest } from "./lib/sse";
   404 // 可选：流式 Markdown 渲染
   405 // import { Streamdown } from "streamdown";
   406 
   407 const supabaseUrl = import.meta.env.VITE_SUPABASE_URL;
   408 const supabaseAnonKey = import.meta.env.VITE_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY;
   409 
   410 export function ChatComponent() {
   411   const [content, setContent] = useState("");
   412   const [isStreaming, setIsStreaming] = useState(false);
   413   const abortRef = useRef<AbortController | null>(null);
   414 
   415   /**
   416    * 发起流式对话请求，逐帧累积模型回复内容。
   417    * @param userMessage - 用户输入的消息文本
   418    */
   419   const handleChat = async (userMessage: string) => {
   420     setContent("");
   421     setIsStreaming(true);
   422     abortRef.current = new AbortController();
   423 
   424     await sendStreamRequest({
   425       functionUrl: `${supabaseUrl}/functions/v1/wenxin-text-generation`,
   426       requestBody: {
   427         messages: [{ role: "user", content: userMessage }],
   428       },
   429       supabaseAnonKey,
   430       onData: (data) => {
   431         if (data === "[DONE]") return;
   432         try {
   433           const parsed = JSON.parse(data);
   434           // 文心大模型 SSE 格式：choices[0].delta.content
   435           const chunk = parsed.choices?.[0]?.delta?.content ?? "";
   436           setContent((prev) => prev + chunk);
   437         } catch {
   438           // 跳过无法解析的帧
   439         }
   440       },
   441       onComplete: () => setIsStreaming(false),
   442       onError: (error) => {
   443         console.error("Stream error:", error);
   444         setIsStreaming(false);
   445       },
   446       signal: abortRef.current.signal,
   447     });
   448   };
   449 
   450   /** 中断正在进行的流式请求 */
   451   const handleAbort = () => {
   452     abortRef.current?.abort();
   453   };
   454 
   455   return (
   456     <div>
   457       <div>{content}</div>
   458       {/* 使用 Streamdown 渲染 Markdown（可选）：
   459       <Streamdown parseIncompleteMarkdown isAnimating={isStreaming}>
   460         {content}
   461       </Streamdown>
   462       */}
   463       {isStreaming && <button onClick={handleAbort}>停止生成</button>}
   464     </div>
   465   );
   466 }
   467 ```

   470 
   471 ### MiniProgram 平台
   472 
   473 依赖安装（使用 pnpm）：
   474 
   475 ```bash
   476 pnpm add miaoda-taro-utils@^0.0.4
   477 ```
   478 
   479 **CRITICAL 注意事项（来自平台验证实现）：**
   480 
   481 - `appId` 必须填入空字符串 `''`，否则会导致无法请求
   482 - `sendChatStream` 的 `endpoint` 从接口 URL 中提取
   483 - 前端传入完整的 `messages`，Edge Function 中仅进行合法性校验，不拼接或修改 messages，确保直接透传到上游 API
   484 - 流式数据结构为：`data: {"id":"as-btb3y1g6iq","choices":[{"index":0,"delta":{"content":"经济"}}]}`
   485 - 使用 `useCallback` 或 `useEffect` 时，避免监听流式数据，以免产生循环
   486 - 需要使用 `@tarojs/components` 中的 `RichText` 来处理模型返回 Markdown 格式的内容展示
   487 
   488 **Taro 小程序端调用示例：**
   489 
   490 ```typescript
   491 import { sendChatStream } from "miaoda-taro-utils/chatStream";
   492 import { useState, useCallback } from "react";
   493 import { RichText } from "@tarojs/components";
   494 
   495 const supabaseUrl = process.env.TARO_APP_SUPABASE_URL;
   496 
   497 export function ChatMiniProgram() {
   498   const [fullContent, setFullContent] = useState("");
   499   const [isStreaming, setIsStreaming] = useState(false);
   500   // 注意：不要在 useEffect 或 useCallback 中监听 fullContent，避免产生循环
   501   const abortRef = useRef<(() => void) | null>(null);
   502 
   503   /**
   504    * 发起小程序端流式对话请求。
   505    * @param userMessage - 用户输入的消息文本
   506    */
   507   const handleChat = useCallback(async (userMessage: string) => {
   508     setFullContent("");
   509     setIsStreaming(true);
   510     let accumulated = "";
   511 
   512     const { abort } = sendChatStream({
   513       endpoint: `${supabaseUrl}/functions/v1/wenxin-text-generation`,
   514       // CRITICAL: appId 必须填空字符串，否则请求失败
   515       appId: "",
   516       messages: [{ role: "user", content: userMessage }],
   517       /**
   518        * @param rawData - 原始流式数据字符串
   519        * 格式示例: {"id":"as-btb3y1g6iq","choices":[{"index":0,"delta":{"content":"内容"}}]}
   520        */
   521       onUpdate: (rawData: string) => {
   522         try {
   523           if (rawData === "[DONE]") return;
   524           const data = JSON.parse(rawData);
   525           const chunk = data.choices?.[0]?.delta?.content ?? "";
   526           accumulated += chunk;
   527           // 使用局部变量累积后统一 setState，避免 closure 陷阱
   528           setFullContent(accumulated);
   529         } catch (e) {
   530           console.error("解析流数据失败:", e);
   531         }
   532       },
   533       onComplete: () => {
   534         setIsStreaming(false);
   535         console.log("回复完成");
   536       },
   537       onError: (error: Error) => {
   538         console.error("回复出错:", error);
   539         setIsStreaming(false);
   540       },
   541     });
   542 
   543     abortRef.current = abort;
   544   }, []); // 注意：依赖项中不包含流式数据，避免产生循环
   545 
   546   /** 中断正在进行的流式请求 */
   547   const handleAbort = () => {
   548     abortRef.current?.();
   549   };
   550 
   551   return (
   552     <View>
   553       {/* 使用 RichText 渲染 Markdown 格式内容 */}
   554       <RichText nodes={fullContent} />
   555       {isStreaming && <Button onClick={handleAbort}>停止生成</Button>}
   556     </View>
   557   );
   558 }
   559 ```

   562 
   563 ### App 平台
   564 
   565 依赖安装：
   566 
   567 ```bash
   568 pnpm add eventsource-parser react-native-marked
   569 ```
   570 
   571 - `expo/fetch`：Expo 内置，无需安装，**必须使用此包而非全局 fetch**（RN 原生 fetch 不支持流式 `response.body`）
   572 - `eventsource-parser`：SSE 事件解析器，纯 JS 实现，兼容 React Native
   573 - `react-native-marked`：Markdown 渲染组件，用于在聊天界面富文本展示 AI 回复
   574 
   575 **SSE 流处理工具函数：**
   576 
   577 ```ts
   578 // utils/sseStream.ts
   579 import { createParser, type EventSourceParser } from 'eventsource-parser';
   580 
   581 export interface SSEOptions {
   582   onData: (data: string) => void;
   583   onCompleted?: (error?: Error) => void;
   584   onAborted?: () => void;
   585 }
   586 
   587 export const processSSEStream = (
   588   signal: AbortSignal | undefined,
   589   response: Response,
   590   options: SSEOptions
   591 ): void => {
   592   const reader = response.body.getReader();
   593   const decoder = new TextDecoder('utf-8');
   594   const parser: EventSourceParser = createParser({
   595     onEvent: (event) => {
   596       if (event.data) {
   597         for (const data of event.data.split('\n')) {
   598           options.onData(data);
   599         }
   600       }
   601     },
   602   });
   603 
   604   const read = (): void => {
   605     reader.read()
   606       .then((result) => {
   607         if (result.done) { return; }
   608         parser.feed(decoder.decode(result.value, { stream: true }));
   609         read();
   610       })
   611       .catch((error: Error) => {
   612         if (signal?.aborted) { options.onAborted?.(); }
   613       });
   614   };
   615 
   616   read();
   617 };
   618 ```
   619 
   620 **通用流式请求函数：**
   621 
   622 ```ts
   623 // utils/streamRequest.ts
   624 import { fetch } from 'expo/fetch';
   625 import { processSSEStream } from './sseStream';
   626 
   627 export const sendStreamRequest = async (options: {
   628   functionUrl: string;
   629   requestBody: any;
   630   supabaseAnonKey: string;
   631   onData: (data: string) => void;
   632   onComplete: () => void;
   633   onError: (error: Error) => void;
   634   signal?: AbortSignal;
   635 }): Promise<void> => {
   636   const { functionUrl, requestBody, supabaseAnonKey, onData, onComplete, onError, signal } = options;
   637 
   638   try {
   639     const response = await fetch(functionUrl, {
   640       method: 'POST',
   641       headers: {
   642         'Authorization': `Bearer ${supabaseAnonKey}`,
   643         'apikey': supabaseAnonKey,
   644         'Content-Type': 'application/json',
   645       },
   646       body: JSON.stringify(requestBody),
   647       signal,
   648     });
   649 
   650     processSSEStream(signal, response, {
   651       onData,
   652       onCompleted: (error) => error ? onError(error) : onComplete(),
   653       onAborted: () => {},
   654     });
   655   } catch (error) {
   656     if (!signal?.aborted) onError(error as Error);
   657   }
   658 };
   659 ```

   123 ## Edge Function 代码
   124 
   125 Edge Function 负责注入平台密钥并转发请求，前端不直接接触 `INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY`。
   126 
   127 Web、MiniProgram 和 App 均可使用同一个 Edge Function，因为响应为标准 JSON（非二进制流）。
   128 
   129 ```typescript
   130 // edge-functions/short-speech-recognition.ts
   131 import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts";
   132 
   133 /**
   134  * Edge Function：短语音识别
   135  * 接收前端传来的 base64 编码语音数据，注入平台密钥后调用上游 API，
   136  * 并将识别结果 JSON 返回给前端。
   137  */
   138 serve(async (req: Request): Promise<Response> => {
   139   if (req.method !== "POST") {
   140     return new Response("Method Not Allowed", { status: 405 });
   141   }
   142 
   143   // --- 解析请求体 ---
   144   let speech: string;
   145   let len: number;
   146   let format: string;
   147   let rate: number;
   148   let cuid: string;
   149 
   150   try {
   151     const body = await req.json();
   152     speech = body.speech;
   153     len = body.len;
   154     format = body.format ?? "wav";
   155     rate = body.rate ?? 16000;
   156     cuid = body.cuid ?? "miaoda-edge-cuid";
   157 
   158     if (!speech) throw new Error("Missing speech");
   159     if (typeof len !== "number" || len <= 0) throw new Error("Missing or invalid len");
   160   } catch {
   161     return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "Invalid request body" }), {
   162       status: 400,
   163       headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
   164     });
   165   }
   166 
   167   // --- 注入平台密钥（严禁暴露到前端） ---
   168   const apiKey = Deno.env.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY");
   169   if (!apiKey) {
   170     return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "Server configuration error" }), {
   171       status: 500,
   172       headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
   173     });
   174   }
   175 
   176   // --- 调用上游 API ---
   177   const upstream = await fetch("https://app-bhs9a5otro5d-api-Aa2PZnjEw5NL-gateway.appmiaoda.com/server_api", {
   178     method: "POST",
   179     headers: {
   180       "Content-Type": "application/json",
   181       "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
   182     },
   183     body: JSON.stringify({ format, rate, cuid, speech, len }),
   184   });
   185 
   186   // 透传配额/余额错误
   187   if (upstream.status === 429 || upstream.status === 402) {
   188     const errText = await upstream.text();
   189     return new Response(errText, {
   190       status: upstream.status,
   191       headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
   192     });
   193   }
   194 
   195   if (!upstream.ok) {
   196     return new Response(
   197       JSON.stringify({ error: `Upstream error: ${upstream.status}` }),
   198       { status: 502, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
   199     );
   200   }
   201 
   202   const data = await upstream.json();
   203   return new Response(JSON.stringify(data), {
   204     status: 200,
   205     headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
   206   });
   207 });
   208 ```

   212 ## 前端调用代码
   213 
   214 ### Web 平台
   215 
   216 Web 端录音时 MediaRecorder 默认产出 `audio/webm`，需先转换为 `audio/wav`（采样率 16000）再进行 base64 编码。
   217 
   218 ```typescript
   219 /**
   220  * 将 Blob 转换为 base64 字符串。
   221  *
   222  * @param blob - 待转换的 Blob 对象
   223  * @returns base64 编码字符串（不含 data URL 前缀）
   224  */
   225 function blobToBase64(blob: Blob): Promise<string> {
   226   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   227     const reader = new FileReader();
   228     reader.onload = () => {
   229       const dataUrl = reader.result as string;
   230       resolve(dataUrl.split(",")[1]); // 去掉 data:audio/wav;base64, 前缀
   231     };
   232     reader.onerror = reject;
   233     reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
   234   });
   235 }
   236 
   237 /**
   238  * 调用 Edge Function 进行短语音识别（Web 端）。
   239  * 注意：录音格式需为 wav，采样率 16000，否则识别率会下降。
   240  *
   241  * @param wavBlob - 转换后的 wav 格式音频 Blob
   242  * @returns 识别出的文字
   243  */
   244 async function recognizeSpeechWeb(wavBlob: Blob): Promise<string> {
   245   const speechBase64 = await blobToBase64(wavBlob);
   246   const len = wavBlob.size;
   247 
   248   const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke("short-speech-recognition", {
   249     body: {
   250       speech: speechBase64,
   251       len,
   252       format: "wav",
   253       rate: 16000,
   254       cuid: "web-user-cuid",
   255     },
   256   });
   257 
   258   if (error) throw error;
   259   if (data.err_no !== 0) throw new Error(`识别失败 ${data.err_no}: ${data.err_msg}`);
   260   return data.result[0] ?? "";
   261 }
   262 ```
   263 
   264 ### App 平台
   265 
   266 App 端使用 `expo-audio` 录音，产出 `audio/m4a` 格式，录音时指定 16000Hz 单声道，无需额外格式转换。
   267 
   268 **录音参数：**
   269 
   270 ```typescript
   271 import { useAudioRecorder, setAudioModeAsync, requestRecordingPermissionsAsync, IOSOutputFormat, AudioQuality } from 'expo-audio';
   272 import type { RecordingOptions } from 'expo-audio';
   273 
   274 const RECORDING_OPTIONS: RecordingOptions = {
   275   extension: '.m4a',
   276   sampleRate: 16000,
   277   numberOfChannels: 1,
   278   bitRate: 64000,
   279   android: { outputFormat: 'mpeg4', audioEncoder: 'aac' },
   280   ios: { outputFormat: IOSOutputFormat.MPEG4AAC, audioQuality: AudioQuality.HIGH, linearPCMBitDepth: 16, linearPCMIsBigEndian: false, linearPCMIsFloat: false },
   281   web: { mimeType: 'audio/webm', bitsPerSecond: 64000 },
   282 };
   283 ```
   284 
   285 **录音 → 识别：**
   286 
   287 ```typescript
   288 // 开始
   289 await setAudioModeAsync({ allowsRecording: true, playsInSilentMode: true });
   290 await recorder.prepareToRecordAsync();
   291 recorder.record();
   292 
   293 // 停止 → 转文字
   294 await recorder.stop();
   295 const transcript = await transcribeAudio(recorder.uri!);
   296 ```
   297 
   298 **transcribeAudio 实现：**
   299 
   300 ```typescript
   301 async function transcribeAudio(fileUri: string): Promise<string> {
   302   const fileResponse = await fetch(fileUri);
   303   const contentType = fileResponse.headers.get('content-type') ?? '';
   304   const rawBuffer = await fileResponse.arrayBuffer();
   305 
   306   const needsConversion = contentType.includes('webm') || fileUri.endsWith('.webm');
   307   const audioBuffer = needsConversion ? await convertToWav(rawBuffer) : rawBuffer;
   308   const format = needsConversion ? 'wav' : 'm4a';
   309   const len = audioBuffer.byteLength;
   310   const speech = arrayBufferToBase64(audioBuffer);
   311 
   312   const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('short-speech-recognition', {
   313     body: { speech, len, format, rate: 16000, cuid: 'app-user' },
   314   });
   315 
   316   if (error || data?.err_no !== 0) throw new Error(data?.err_msg || '语音识别失败');
   317   return data.result[0] ?? '';
   318 }
   319 ```
   320 
   321 **convertToWav（Web fallback 场景使用）：**
   322 
   323 ```typescript
   324 async function convertToWav(arrayBuffer: ArrayBuffer): Promise<ArrayBuffer> {
   325   const audioCtx = new AudioContext({ sampleRate: 16000 });
   326   const audioBuffer = await audioCtx.decodeAudioData(arrayBuffer);
   327   const pcm = audioBuffer.getChannelData(0);
   328   await audioCtx.close();
   329 
   330   const wav = new ArrayBuffer(44 + pcm.length * 2);
   331   const v = new DataView(wav);
   332   const w = (o: number, s: string) => { for (let i = 0; i < s.length; i++) v.setUint8(o + i, s.charCodeAt(i)); };
   333   w(0, 'RIFF'); v.setUint32(4, 36 + pcm.length * 2, true); w(8, 'WAVE');
   334   w(12, 'fmt '); v.setUint32(16, 16, true); v.setUint16(20, 1, true); v.setUint16(22, 1, true);
   335   v.setUint32(24, 16000, true); v.setUint32(28, 32000, true); v.setUint16(32, 2, true); v.setUint16(34, 16, true);
   336   w(36, 'data'); v.setUint32(40, pcm.length * 2, true);
   337   for (let i = 0; i < pcm.length; i++) {
   338     const s = Math.max(-1, Math.min(1, pcm[i]));
   339     v.setInt16(44 + i * 2, s < 0 ? s * 0x8000 : s * 0x7fff, true);
   340   }
   341   return wav;
   342 }
   343 ```
   344 
   345 ### MiniProgram 平台
   346 
   347 MiniProgram 端原生录音产出 `audio/x-m4a` 格式，无需格式转换，直接读取文件内容并 base64 编码。
   348 
   349 ```typescript
   350 /**
   351  * 调用 Edge Function 进行短语音识别（MiniProgram 端）。
   352  * 使用 Taro.getFileSystemManager 读取录音文件并转为 base64。
   353  *
   354  * @param m4aFilePath - 录音文件的临时路径（x-m4a 格式）
   355  * @returns 识别出的文字
   356  */
   357 async function recognizeSpeechMiniProgram(m4aFilePath: string): Promise<string> {
   358   // 读取文件并获取 base64 和字节数
   359   const speechBase64: string = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   360     Taro.getFileSystemManager().readFile({
   361       filePath: m4aFilePath,
   362       encoding: "base64",
   363       success: (res) => resolve(res.data as string),
   364       fail: (err) => reject(new Error(JSON.stringify(err))),
   365     });
   366   });
   367 
   368   // 获取原始字节数（用于 len 参数）
   369   const fileInfo: Taro.getFileInfo.SuccessCallbackResult = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   370     Taro.getFileSystemManager().getFileInfo({
   371       filePath: m4aFilePath,
   372       success: resolve,
   373       fail: (err) => reject(new Error(JSON.stringify(err))),
   374     });
   375   });
   376 
   377   const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke("short-speech-recognition", {
   378     body: {
   379       speech: speechBase64,
   380       len: fileInfo.size,
   381       format: "m4a",
   382       rate: 16000,
   383       cuid: "miniprogram-user-cuid",
   384     },
   385   });
   386 
   387   if (error) throw error;
   388   if (data.err_no !== 0) throw new Error(`识别失败 ${data.err_no}: ${data.err_msg}`);
   389   return data.result[0] ?? "";
   390 }
   391 ```
   392 
   393 ---
   394 
   395 ## 注意事项
   396 
   397 1. **密钥安全**：`INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY` 仅可在 Edge Function 服务端读取，严禁暴露到前端代码或客户端日志中。
   398 
   399 2. **错误处理**：务必处理以下错误场景：
   400    - HTTP 429（配额超限）：提示用户稍后重试
   401    - HTTP 402（余额不足）：提示充值
   402    - `err_no !== 0`（业务错误）：根据错误码提示用户，常见原因包括音频质量差（3301）、格式不支持、时长超限
   403 
   404 3. **计费**：
   405    - 计费信息以平台实际配置为准
   406    - 避免在循环或高频场景中重复调用，每次请求均计费
   407 
   408 4. **录音格式转换（Web）**：
   409    - MediaRecorder 默认录制格式为 `audio/webm`，**必须**转换为 `audio/wav` 后才能传给此 API
   410    - 录音时需确保采样率设置为 16000 Hz
   411    - 推荐使用 `AudioContext` + `ScriptProcessorNode` 或第三方库（如 `lamejs`、`recordrtc`）完成格式转换
   412 
   413 5. **len 参数**：传递的是语音文件**原始字节数**（即 `Blob.size`），不是 base64 字符串的长度。
   414 
   415 6. **cuid 参数**：建议传入设备唯一标识（MAC 地址、设备 ID 等），用于问题排查和用量统计，长度不超过 60 字符。
   416 
   417 7. **语音质量要求**：
   418    - 格式：wav（不压缩，PCM 编码）或 m4a
   419    - 位深：16bit，单声道
   420    - 时长：不超过 60 秒
   421    - 环境噪声过大会导致 `err_no: 3301`（音频质量过差）
   422 


</observation>

**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-bhs9a5otro5d/src/pages/enterprise/Messages.tsx]
Thought: 原因很清楚：**联系人列表只查 messages 表里已有往来记录的用户，但 messages 表是空的**，所以页面显示"暂无消息往来"，企业无法发起任何对话。

修复方案：以**投递了该企业职位的求职者**作为候选人列表，即使还没有消息记录也能直接点击发起沟通。
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
import React, { useEffect, useState, useRef } from 'react';
import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
import { Message } from '@/types/types';
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Avatar, AvatarFallback } from '@/components/ui/avatar';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';
import { Skeleton } from '@/components/ui/skeleton';
import { MessageSquare, Send } from 'lucide-react';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

interface Contact {
  id: string;
  display_name?: string;
  username?: string;
  lastMessage?: string;
  unread?: number;
}

export default function EnterpriseMessages() {
  const { user } = useAuth();
  const [contacts, setContacts] = useState<Contact[]>([]);
  const [selectedContact, setSelectedContact] = useState<Contact | null>(null);
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([]);
  const [inputText, setInputText] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [sending, setSending] = useState(false);
  const messagesEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (user) fetchContacts();
  }, [user]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (selectedContact) fetchMessages(selectedContact.id);
  }, [selectedContact]);

  useEffect(() => {
    messagesEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
  }, [messages]);

  const fetchContacts = async () => {
    // 获取与当前企业有消息往来的用户
    const { data } = await supabase
      .from('messages')
      .select('sender_id, receiver_id, content, created_at')
      .or(`sender_id.eq.${user!.id},receiver_id.eq.${user!.id}`)
      .order('created_at', { ascending: false });

    if (!Array.isArray(data)) { setLoading(false); return; }

    // 提取联系人ID
    const contactIds = new Set<string>();
    data.forEach((m: { sender_id: string; receiver_id: string }) => {
      if (m.sender_id !== user!.id) contactIds.add(m.sender_id);
      if (m.receiver_id !== user!.id) contactIds.add(m.receiver_id);
    });

    if (contactIds.size === 0) { setLoading(false); return; }

    const { data: profiles } = await supabase
      .from('profiles')
      .select('id, display_name, username')
      .in('id', Array.from(contactIds));

    setContacts(Array.isArray(profiles) ? profiles.map(p => ({
      id: p.id,
      display_name: p.display_name,
      username: p.username,
      lastMessage: data.find((m: { sender_id: string; receiver_id: string }) => m.sender_id === p.id || m.receiver_id === p.id)?.content,
    })) : []);
    setLoading(false);
  };

  const fetchMessages = async (contactId: string) => {
    const { data } = await supabase
      .from('messages')
      .select('*')
      .or(`and(sender_id.eq.${user!.id},receiver_id.eq.${contactId}),and(sender_id.eq.${contactId},receiver_id.eq.${user!.id})`)
      .order('created_at', { ascending: true })
      .limit(50);
    setMessages(Array.isArray(data) ? data as Message[] : []);
  };

  const handleSend = async () => {
    if (!inputText.trim() || !selectedContact || sending) return;
    setSending(true);
    const { error } = await supabase.from('messages').insert({
      sender_id: user!.id,
      receiver_id: selectedContact.id,
      content: inputText.trim(),
    });
    if (error) toast.error('发送失败');
    else {
      setInputText('');
      fetchMessages(selectedContact.id);
    }
    setSending(false);
  };

  return (
    <div className="max-w-5xl mx-auto px-4 md:px-8 py-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-foreground mb-6 text-balance">沟通协作</h1>

      <div className="flex gap-4 h-[600px]">
        {/* 联系人列表 */}
        <Card className="w-56 shrink-0 flex flex-col hidden md:flex">
          <CardHeader className="pb-3 shrink-0">
            <CardTitle className="text-sm">候选人列表</CardTitle>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent className="p-0 flex-1 overflow-hidden">
            <ScrollArea className="h-full">
              {loading ? (
                <div className="p-3 space-y-2">{Array(4).fill(0).map((_, i) => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-12 bg-muted" />)}</div>
              ) : contacts.length === 0 ? (
                <div className="p-4 text-center text-xs text-muted-foreground">暂无消息往来</div>
              ) : (
                <div className="p-2 space-y-1">
                  {contacts.map(contact => (
                    <button
                      key={contact.id}
                      onClick={() => setSelectedContact(contact)}
                      className={`w-full text-left p-2.5 rounded-md transition-colors flex items-center gap-2 ${
                        selectedContact?.id === contact.id ? 'bg-primary/10' : 'hover:bg-muted'
                      }`}
                    >
                      <Avatar className="w-8 h-8 shrink-0">
                        <AvatarFallback className="text-xs bg-muted-foreground/20">
                          {(contact.display_name || contact.username || '?')[0].toUpperCase()}
                        </AvatarFallback>
                      </Avatar>
                      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                        <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate">
                          {contact.display_name || contact.username}
                        </p>
                        {contact.lastMessage && (
                          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">{contact.lastMessage}</p>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </ScrollArea>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        {/* 消息区域 */}
        <Card className="flex-1 min-w-0 flex flex-col">
          {!selectedContact ? (
            <CardContent className="flex-1 flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-3 text-muted-foreground">
              <MessageSquare className="w-12 h-12 opacity-30" />
              <p className="text-sm">选择一位候选人开始沟通</p>
            </CardContent>
          ) : (
            <>
              <CardHeader className="pb-3 shrink-0 border-b border-border">
                <CardTitle className="text-base flex items-center gap-2">
                  <Avatar className="w-7 h-7">
                    <AvatarFallback className="text-xs bg-primary text-primary-foreground">
                      {(selectedContact.display_name || selectedContact.username || '?')[0].toUpperCase()}
                    </AvatarFallback>
                  </Avatar>
                  {selectedContact.display_name || selectedContact.username}
                </CardTitle>
              </CardHeader>
              <CardContent className="flex-1 min-h-0 p-0 flex flex-col">
                <ScrollArea className="flex-1">
                  <div className="p-4 space-y-4">
                    {messages.length === 0 && (

                      <div key={msg.id} className={`flex ${msg.sender_id === user!.id ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>
                        <div className={`max-w-[70%] rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm ${
                          msg.sender_id === user!.id
                            ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground'
                            : 'bg-muted text-foreground'

New String: ```
import React, { useEffect, useState, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
import { Message } from '@/types/types';
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Avatar, AvatarFallback } from '@/components/ui/avatar';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';
import { Skeleton } from '@/components/ui/skeleton';
import { MessageSquare, Send, Users } from 'lucide-react';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

interface Contact {
  id: string;
  display_name?: string;
  username?: string;
  jobTitle?: string;   // 投递的职位名称
  lastMessage?: string;
  hasMessage: boolean; // 是否已有消息往来
}

export default function EnterpriseMessages() {
  const { user } = useAuth();
  const [contacts, setContacts] = useState<Contact[]>([]);
  const [selectedContact, setSelectedContact] = useState<Contact | null>(null);
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([]);
  const [inputText, setInputText] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [sending, setSending] = useState(false);
  const messagesEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  const fetchContacts = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!user) return;
    setLoading(true);

    // 1. 获取该企业发布的所有职位 ID
    const { data: jobs } = await supabase
      .from('jobs')
      .select('id, title')
      .eq('enterprise_id', user.id);

    const jobMap: Record<string, string> = {};
    (jobs ?? []).forEach((j: { id: string; title: string }) => { jobMap[j.id] = j.title; });
    const jobIds = Object.keys(jobMap);

    // 2. 获取投递了这些职位的求职者 ID
    const applicantMap: Record<string, string> = {}; // applicant_id → job title
    if (jobIds.length > 0) {
      const { data: apps } = await supabase
        .from('applications')
        .select('applicant_id, job_id')
        .in('job_id', jobIds);
      (apps ?? []).forEach((a: { applicant_id: string; job_id: string }) => {
        if (!applicantMap[a.applicant_id]) {
          applicantMap[a.applicant_id] = jobMap[a.job_id] ?? '';
        }
      });
    }

    // 3. 获取已有消息往来的联系人 ID
    const { data: msgData } = await supabase
      .from('messages')
      .select('sender_id, receiver_id, content, created_at')
      .or(`sender_id.eq.${user.id},receiver_id.eq.${user.id}`)
      .order('created_at', { ascending: false });

    const msgContactIds = new Set<string>();
    const lastMsgMap: Record<string, string> = {};
    (msgData ?? []).forEach((m: { sender_id: string; receiver_id: string; content: string }) => {
      const otherId = m.sender_id === user.id ? m.receiver_id : m.sender_id;
      if (!lastMsgMap[otherId]) lastMsgMap[otherId] = m.content;
      msgContactIds.add(otherId);
    });

    // 4. 合并所有联系人 ID（投递者 + 有消息往来的）
    const allIds = new Set([...Object.keys(applicantMap), ...msgContactIds]);
    if (allIds.size === 0) { setLoading(false); return; }

    // 5. 获取 profile 信息
    const { data: profiles } = await supabase
      .from('profiles')
      .select('id, display_name, username')
      .in('id', Array.from(allIds));

    const contactList: Contact[] = (profiles ?? []).map((p: { id: string; display_name?: string; username?: string }) => ({
      id: p.id,
      display_name: p.display_name,
      username: p.username,
      jobTitle: applicantMap[p.id],
      lastMessage: lastMsgMap[p.id],
      hasMessage: msgContactIds.has(p.id),
    }));

    // 有消息的排前面，再按名字排序
    contactList.sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.hasMessage !== b.hasMessage) return a.hasMessage ? -1 : 1;
      return (a.display_name || a.username || '').localeCompare(b.display_name || b.username || '');
    });

    setContacts(contactList);
    setLoading(false);
  }, [user]);

  useEffect(() => { fetchContacts(); }, [fetchContacts]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (selectedContact) fetchMessages(selectedContact.id);
  }, [selectedContact]);

  useEffect(() => {
    messagesEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
  }, [messages]);

  const fetchMessages = async (contactId: string) => {
    const { data } = await supabase
      .from('messages')
      .select('*')
      .or(`and(sender_id.eq.${user!.id},receiver_id.eq.${contactId}),and(sender_id.eq.${contactId},receiver_id.eq.${user!.id})`)
      .order('created_at', { ascending: true })
      .limit(100);
    setMessages(Array.isArray(data) ? data as Message[] : []);
  };

  const handleSend = async () => {
    if (!inputText.trim() || !selectedContact || sending) return;
    setSending(true);
    const { error } = await supabase.from('messages').insert({
      sender_id: user!.id,
      receiver_id: selectedContact.id,
      content: inputText.trim(),
    });
    if (error) {
      toast.error('发送失败');
    } else {
      setInputText('');
      await fetchMessages(selectedContact.id);
      // 更新联系人列表中的最后消息
      setContacts(prev => prev.map(c =>
        c.id === selectedContact.id
          ? { ...c, lastMessage: inputText.trim(), hasMessage: true }
          : c
      ));
    }
    setSending(false);
  };

  return (
    <div className="max-w-5xl mx-auto px-4 md:px-8 py-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-foreground mb-6 text-balance">沟通协作</h1>

      <div className="flex gap-4 h-[600px]">
        {/* 候选人列表 */}
        <Card className="w-64 shrink-0 hidden md:flex flex-col">
          <CardHeader className="pb-3 shrink-0 border-b border-border">
            <CardTitle className="text-sm flex items-center gap-2">
              <Users className="w-4 h-4 text-primary" />
              候选人列表
              {!loading && contacts.length > 0 && (
                <Badge variant="secondary" className="ml-auto text-xs">{contacts.length}</Badge>
              )}
            </CardTitle>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent className="p-0 flex-1 overflow-hidden">
            <ScrollArea className="h-full">
              {loading ? (
                <div className="p-3 space-y-2">
                  {Array(5).fill(0).map((_, i) => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-14 bg-muted" />)}
                </div>
              ) : contacts.length === 0 ? (
                <div className="p-6 text-center space-y-2">
                  <Users className="w-8 h-8 text-muted-foreground/40 mx-auto" />
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">暂无候选人</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground/60">发布职位后，投递者将显示在此处</p>
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className="p-2 space-y-0.5">
                  {contacts.map(contact => (
                    <button
                      key={contact.id}
                      onClick={() => setSelectedContact(contact)}
                      className={`w-full text-left p-2.5 rounded-md transition-colors flex items-start gap-2.5 ${
                        selectedContact?.id === contact.id
                          ? 'bg-primary/10 border border-primary/20'
                          : 'hover:bg-muted border border-transparent'
                      }`}
                    >
                      <Avatar className="w-8 h-8 shrink-0 mt-0.5">
                        <AvatarFallback className={`text-xs ${selectedContact?.id === contact.id ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground' : 'bg-muted-foreground/20'}`}>
                          {(contact.display_name || contact.username || '?')[0].toUpperCase()}
                        </AvatarFallback>
                      </Avatar>
                      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
                          <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate">
                            {contact.display_name || contact.username}
                          </p>
                          {contact.hasMessage && (
                            <span className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-primary shrink-0" />
                          )}
                        </div>
                        {contact.jobTitle && (
                          <p className="text-xs text-primary/70 truncate">投递：{contact.jobTitle}</p>
                        )}
                        {contact.lastMessage && (
                          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">{contact.lastMessage}</p>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </ScrollArea>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        {/* 消息区域 */}
        <Card className="flex-1 min-w-0 flex flex-col">
          {!selectedContact ? (
            <CardContent className="flex-1 flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-3 text-muted-foreground p-8">
              <MessageSquare className="w-12 h-12 opacity-20" />
              <p className="text-sm font-medium">选择一位候选人开始沟通</p>
              <p className="text-xs opacity-60 text-center text-pretty">
                左侧列表包含所有投递了贵司职位的候选人，点击即可发起沟通
              </p>
            </CardContent>
          ) : (
            <>
              <CardHeader className="pb-3 shrink-0 border-b border-border">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <Avatar className="w-8 h-8">
                    <AvatarFallback className="text-xs bg-primary text-primary-foreground">
                      {(selectedContact.display_name || selectedContact.username || '?')[0].toUpperCase()}
                    </AvatarFallback>
                  </Avatar>
                  <div className="min-w-0">
                    <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-foreground truncate">
                      {selectedContact.display_name || selectedContact.username}
                    </p>
                    {selectedContact.jobTitle && (
                      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">投递职位：{selectedContact.jobTitle}</p>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </CardHeader>
              <CardContent className="flex-1 min-h-0 p-0 flex flex-col">
                <ScrollArea className="flex-1">
                  <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
                    {messages.length === 0 && (
                      <div className="text-center py-10">
                        <MessageSquare className="w-8 h-8 text-muted-foreground/30 mx-auto mb-2" />
                        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">还没有消息，发送第一条消息开始沟通吧</p>
                      </div>
                    )}
                    {messages.map(msg => (
                      <div key={msg.id} className={`flex ${msg.sender_id === user!.id ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>
                        <div className={`max-w-[70%] rounded-2xl px-3.5 py-2 text-sm leading-relaxed ${
                          msg.sender_id === user!.id
                            ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground rounded-tr-sm'
                            : 'bg-muted text-foreground rounded-tl-sm'
                        }`}>
                          {msg.content}
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                    <div ref={messagesEndRef} />
                  </div>
                </ScrollArea>
                <div className="p-3 border-t border-border shrink-0 bg-background/50">
                  <div className="flex gap-2">
                    <Input
                      placeholder="输入消息，按 Enter 发送..."
                      value={inputText}
                      onChange={e => setInputText(e.target.value)}
                      onKeyDown={e => { if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) { e.preventDefault(); handleSend(); } }}
                      className="flex-1 px-3"
                      disabled={sending}
                    />
                    <Button
                      size="icon"
                      className="shrink-0 h-9 w-9"
                      onClick={handleSend}
                      disabled={sending || !inputText.trim()}
                    >
                      <Send className="w-4 h-4" />
                    </Button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </CardContent>
            </>
          )}
        </Card>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

<action>
**MessageAction** (source=EventSource.AGENT)
CONTENT: 0 错误。

---

**根本原因**：原来的联系人列表**只从 `messages` 表里找有过往来的人**——但 `messages` 表是空的，所以列表一片空白，企业根本无法主动发起对话。

**修复内容**：

| | 修复前 | 修复后 |
|---|---|---|
| 联系人来源 | 仅已有消息记录的人 | **投递了本企业职位的所有求职者** + 已有消息往来的人 |
| 空状态 | "暂无消息往来" 无法操作 | 提示"发布职位后投递者将显示在此处" |
| 候选人信息 | 只显示姓名 | 显示姓名 + **投递的职位名称** |
| 排序 | 无 | 有消息往来的排前，其余按姓名排序 |

现在只要企业发布了职位、有求职者投递，对应的候选人就会出现在沟通列表中，点击即可直接发起对话。
</action>
<action>
**MessageAction** (source=EventSource.USER)
CONTENT: 企业可在“沟通协作”界面，与候选人进行实时沟通，智能体自动解析双方意图，提供标准化回复模板（如面试安排、薪资谈判），或生成个性化建议。支持语音转文字、多语言翻译等功能，提升跨地域沟通效率。

Thought: 
Command: create
Created File with Text:
```
/**
 * Edge Function: chat-ai-assist
 * 智能沟通辅助：分析对话意图 + 生成标准化回复模板 / 个性化建议（SSE 流式）
 */
const corsHeaders = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type",
};

Deno.serve(async (req: Request): Promise<Response> => {
  if (req.method === "OPTIONS") {
    return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders });
  }
  if (req.method !== "POST") {
    return new Response("Method Not Allowed", { status: 405, headers: corsHeaders });
  }

  let messages: Array<{ role: string; content: string }>;
  let mode: string;
  let context: string;

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    messages = body.messages;
    mode = body.mode ?? "suggest"; // "suggest" | "template" | "analyze"
    context = body.context ?? "";
    if (!messages || !Array.isArray(messages) || messages.length === 0) {
      throw new Error("Missing messages");
    }
  } catch (err) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: `Invalid request: ${(err as Error).message}` }),
      { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  const apiKey = Deno.env.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY");
  if (!apiKey) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: "Server configuration error" }),
      { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  // 根据模式构造系统提示
  const systemPrompts: Record<string, string> = {
    suggest: `你是一名专业的HR招聘沟通顾问。请分析当前对话内容，识别候选人意图（如薪资期望、面试时间、岗位疑问等），并为企业HR提供3-5条简洁的个性化回复建议，每条建议前加"•"。回复要专业、友善、简洁。${context ? `\n\n岗位背景：${context}` : ""}`,
    template: `你是一名专业的HR招聘助手。请根据对话场景，生成标准化的HR回复模板。模板类型包括：面试邀约、薪资谈判、岗位说明、拒绝婉拒、录用通知。每个模板用【模板名称】开头，内容清晰专业。${context ? `\n\n岗位背景：${context}` : ""}`,
    analyze: `你是一名HR招聘分析师。请分析候选人的最近一条消息，识别：1.主要意图 2.情绪倾向（积极/中性/消极）3.关注重点 4.建议HR下一步行动。格式简洁，每项单独一行。`,
  };

  const systemContent = systemPrompts[mode] ?? systemPrompts.suggest;
  const fullMessages = [
    { role: "system", content: systemContent },
    ...messages,
  ];

  const upstream = await fetch(
    "https://app-bhs9a5otro5d-api-zYkZz8qovQ1L-gateway.appmiaoda.com/v2/chat/completions",
    {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ messages: fullMessages, enable_thinking: false }),
    }
  );

  if (upstream.status === 429 || upstream.status === 402) {
    const errText = await upstream.text();
    return new Response(errText, {
      status: upstream.status,
      headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }

  if (!upstream.ok || !upstream.body) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: `Upstream error: ${upstream.status}` }),
      { status: 502, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  return new Response(upstream.body, {
    headers: {
      ...corsHeaders,
      "Content-Type": "text/event-stream",
      "Cache-Control": "no-cache",
      "Connection": "keep-alive",
    },
  });
});

```

Created File with Text:
```
/**
 * Edge Function: text-translation
 * 多语言翻译（百度翻译通用版，支持200+语言）
 */
const corsHeaders = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type",
};

Deno.serve(async (req: Request): Promise<Response> => {
  if (req.method === "OPTIONS") {
    return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders });
  }
  if (req.method !== "POST") {
    return new Response("Method Not Allowed", { status: 405, headers: corsHeaders });
  }

  let q: string;
  let from: string;
  let to: string;

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    q = body.q;
    from = body.from ?? "auto";
    to = body.to;
    if (!q) throw new Error("Missing q");
    if (!to) throw new Error("Missing to");
  } catch (err) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: `Invalid request: ${(err as Error).message}` }),
      { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  const apiKey = Deno.env.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY");
  if (!apiKey) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: "Server configuration error" }),
      { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  const upstream = await fetch(
    "https://app-bhs9a5otro5d-api-e94GZ5j0PWpa-gateway.appmiaoda.com/rpc/2.0/mt/texttrans/v1",
    {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json;charset=utf-8",
        "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ q, from, to }),
    }
  );

  if (upstream.status === 429 || upstream.status === 402) {
    const errText = await upstream.text();
    return new Response(errText, {
      status: upstream.status,
      headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }

  if (!upstream.ok) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: `Upstream error: ${upstream.status}` }),
      { status: 502, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  const data = await upstream.json();
  return new Response(JSON.stringify(data), {
    status: 200,
    headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
  });
});

```

</action>

```
/**
 * Edge Function: short-speech-recognition
 * 短语音识别（百度语音识别，支持wav/m4a，最长60秒）
 */
const corsHeaders = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type",
};

Deno.serve(async (req: Request): Promise<Response> => {
  if (req.method === "OPTIONS") {
    return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders });
  }
  if (req.method !== "POST") {
    return new Response("Method Not Allowed", { status: 405, headers: corsHeaders });
  }

  let speech: string;
  let len: number;
  let format: string;
  let rate: number;
  let cuid: string;

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    speech = body.speech;
    len = body.len;
    format = body.format ?? "wav";
    rate = body.rate ?? 16000;
    cuid = body.cuid ?? "miaoda-edge-cuid";
    if (!speech) throw new Error("Missing speech");
    if (typeof len !== "number" || len <= 0) throw new Error("Missing or invalid len");
  } catch (err) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: `Invalid request: ${(err as Error).message}` }),
      { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  const apiKey = Deno.env.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY");
  if (!apiKey) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: "Server configuration error" }),
      { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  const upstream = await fetch(
    "https://app-bhs9a5otro5d-api-Aa2PZnjEw5NL-gateway.appmiaoda.com/server_api",
    {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ format, rate, cuid, speech, len }),
    }
  );

  if (upstream.status === 429 || upstream.status === 402) {
    const errText = await upstream.text();
    return new Response(errText, {
      status: upstream.status,
      headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }

  if (!upstream.ok) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: `Upstream error: ${upstream.status}` }),
      { status: 502, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  const data = await upstream.json();
  return new Response(JSON.stringify(data), {
    status: 200,
    headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
  });
});

```

</action>

```
/**
 * SSE 工具函数 — 用于接收 Edge Function 的流式响应
 * 仅适用于 Web 平台（ky + eventsource-parser）
 */
import ky, { type AfterResponseHook } from 'ky';
import { createParser } from 'eventsource-parser';

export interface StreamRequestOptions {
  /** Edge Function 完整 URL */
  functionUrl: string;
  /** 请求体 */
  requestBody: unknown;
  /** Supabase anon key */
  supabaseAnonKey: string;
  /** 每帧 SSE 数据回调 */
  onData: (data: string) => void;
  /** 完成回调 */
  onComplete: () => void;
  /** 错误回调 */
  onError: (error: Error) => void;
  /** AbortSignal */
  signal?: AbortSignal;
}

/** 发送流式请求到 Supabase Edge Function（SSE 透传模式） */
export async function sendStreamRequest(options: StreamRequestOptions): Promise<void> {
  const { functionUrl, requestBody, supabaseAnonKey, onData, onComplete, onError, signal } = options;

  const sseHook: AfterResponseHook = async (_req, _opts, response) => {
    if (!response.ok || !response.body) return;
    let completed = false;
    const finish = (err?: Error) => {
      if (completed) return;
      completed = true;
      err ? onError(err) : onComplete();
    };

    const reader = response.body.getReader();
    const decoder = new TextDecoder('utf-8');
    const parser = createParser({
      onEvent: (event) => {
        if (event.data) onData(event.data);
      },
    });

    const read = (): void => {
      reader.read().then(({ done, value }) => {
        if (done) { finish(); return; }
        parser.feed(decoder.decode(value, { stream: true }));
        read();
      }).catch((err: Error) => {
        if (signal?.aborted) return;
        finish(err);
      });
    };
    read();
    return response;
  };

  try {
    await ky.post(functionUrl, {
      json: requestBody,
      headers: {
        Authorization: `Bearer ${supabaseAnonKey}`,
        apikey: supabaseAnonKey,
      },
      signal,
      timeout: 30000,
      hooks: { afterResponse: [sseHook] },
    });
  } catch (err) {
    if (!signal?.aborted) onError(err as Error);
  }
}

```
